<p>Other
than
these
few
performances,
no
concerts
or
tours
were
arranged
to
promote
<i>Med&uacute;lla</i>.
Bj&ouml;rk
said
in
numerous
interviews
that
this
was
because
she
wished
to
immediately
continue
writing
and
recording
yet
another
new
album.
She
spoke
to
<i><a
href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rolling
Stone">Rolling
Stone</a></i>
in
June
2004:
&quot;Every
album
I've
done,
the
minute
that
it's
done,
I
feel
really
lubricated
and,
like,
'Wow,
now
I
can
write
an
album
in
five
minutes'...
And
I
just
want
to
find
out
if
that's
just
a
<a
href="/wiki/Fantasy_(psychology)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Fantasy
(psychology)">fantasy</a>
or
if
it's
true.&quot;
Also,
Bj&ouml;rk
thought
it
would
be
too
difficult
to
play
the
songs
live.<sup
id="cite_ref-33"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-33"><span>[</span>33<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
2006,
Bj&ouml;rk
remastered
her
first
three
solo
studio
albums
(<i>Debut</i>,
<i>Post</i>,
<i>Homogenic</i>)
and
her
two
soundtrack
albums
(<i>Selmasongs</i>
and
<i>Drawing
Restraint
9</i>)
in
5.1
surround
sound
for
a
re-issue
in
a
new
box-set
titled
<i><a
href="/wiki/Surrounded?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Surrounded">Surrounded</a></i>,
released
on
27
June.
<i>Vespertine</i>
and
<i>Med&uacute;lla</i>
were
already
available
in
5.1
as
either
DVD-A
or
SACD
but
are
also
included
in
the
box
set
in
repackaged
format.
The
<a
href="/wiki/DualDisc?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="DualDisc">DualDiscs</a>
were
also
released
separately.<sup
id="cite_ref-34"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-34"><span>[</span>34<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>During
this
era,
Bj&ouml;rk
earned
another
<a
href="/wiki/BRIT_Awards?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="BRIT
Awards"
class="mw-redirect">BRIT
Awards</a>
nomination
for
Best
International
Female
Solo
Artist.<sup
id="cite_ref-35"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-35"><span>[</span>35<span>]</span></a></sup>
She
was
also
awarded
the
Inspiration
Award
at
the
Annual
<i><a
href="/wiki/Q_magazine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Q
magazine">Q
Magazine</a></i>
Awards
in
October
2005,
accepting
the
prize
from
Robert
Wyatt,
with
whom
she
collaborated
on
<i>Med&uacute;lla</i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-36"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-36"><span>[</span>36<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk's
former
band,
the
Sugarcubes,
reunited
for
a
one-night-only
concert
in
Reykjav&iacute;k
on
17
November
2006.
Profits
from
the
concert
were
donated
to
the
Sugarcubes'
former
label,
<a
href="/wiki/Smekkleysa?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Smekkleysa"
class="mw-redirect">Smekkleysa</a>,
who
according
to
Bj&ouml;rk's
press
statement,
&quot;continue
to
work
on
a
non-profit
basis
for
the
future
betterment
of
Icelandic
music&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-37"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-37"><span>[</span>37<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<p>Bj&ouml;rk
contributed
a
cover
of
<a
href="/wiki/Joni_Mitchell?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"

Mitchell</a>'s
song
&quot;The
Boho
Dance&quot;
to
the
tribute
album
<i><a

onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="A
Tribute
to
Joni
Mitchell">A
Tribute
to
Joni
Mitchell</a></i>,
released
on
24
April
2007.</p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk's
sixth
full-length
studio
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Volta_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Volta
(album)">Volta</a></i>,
was
released
on
7
May
2007.
It
features
10
tracks
primarily
written
and
produced
by
Bj&ouml;rk
herself
and
is
intended
as
more
direct
and
extroverted
than
her
past
few
albums
but
features
a
wide
range
of
collaborators
and
cross-cultural
musical
elements.
<i>Volta</i>
features
input
from
acclaimed
hip
hop
producer
<a
href="/wiki/Timbaland?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Timbaland">Timbaland</a>,
singer
<a
href="/wiki/Antony_Hegarty?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Antony
Hegarty">Antony
Hegarty</a>,
poet
<a
href="/wiki/Sj%C3%B3n?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sj&oacute;n">Sj&oacute;n</a>,
electronic
beat
programmer
<a
href="/wiki/Mark_Bell_(British_musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mark
Bell
(British
musician)">Mark
Bell</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Kora_(instrument)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kora
(instrument)">kora</a>
master
<a
href="/wiki/Toumani_Diabat%C3%A9?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Toumani
Diabat&eacute;">Toumani
Diabat&eacute;</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Pipa?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pipa">pipa</a>
player
<a
href="/wiki/Min_Xiaofen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Min
Xiaofen">Min
Xiaofen</a>,
and,
on
several
songs,
an
all-female
ensemble
from
Iceland
performing
<a
href="/wiki/Brass?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Brass">brass</a>
compositions.
It
also
uses
the
<a
href="/wiki/Reactable?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Reactable">Reactable</a>,
a
novel
&quot;tangible-interface&quot;
synthesizer
from
the
<a
href="/wiki/Universitat_Pompeu_Fabra?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Universitat
Pompeu
Fabra"
class="mw-redirect">Universitat
Pompeu
Fabra</a>
in
<a
href="/wiki/Barcelona?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Barcelona">Barcelona</a>,
which
on
<i>Volta</i>
is
played
by
Damian
Taylor.</p>








<p>The
first
single
from
the
album,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Earth_Intruders?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Earth
Intruders">Earth
Intruders</a>&quot;,
was
released
digitally
on
9
April
2007
and
became
her
second-ever
<a
href="/wiki/Billboard_Hot_100?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billboard
Hot
100"><i>Billboard</i>
Hot
100</a>
entry
in
the
United
States.
<i>Volta</i>
debuted
at
number
nine
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/Billboard_200?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billboard
200"><i>Billboard</i>
200</a>
albums
chart,
becoming
her
first
top
10
album
in
the
US,
netting
week-one
sales
of
43,000.
The
album
also
reached
number
three
on
the
French
albums
chart
with
sales
of
20,600
albums
sold
in
its
first
week,
and
number
seven
in
the
<a
href="/wiki/UK_Albums_Chart?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="UK
Albums
Chart">UK
Albums
Chart</a>
with
20,456
units
sold.
The
second
single
from
the
album,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Innocence_(Bj%C3%B6rk_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Innocence
(Bj&ouml;rk
song)">Innocence</a>&quot;,
was
digitally
released
on
23
July
2007,
with
an
accompanying
music
video
chosen
from
a
contest
conducted
through
her
official
website.
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Declare_Independence?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Declare
Independence">Declare
Independence</a>&quot;
was
released
on
1
January
2008
in
a
super
deluxe
package
including
two
12&quot;
vinyls,
a
CD,
and
a
DVD
featuring
Oscar-winning
French
director
<a
href="/wiki/Michel_Gondry?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Michel
Gondry">Michel
Gondry</a>'s
&quot;Declare
Independence&quot;
video.<sup
id="cite_ref-38"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-38"><span>[</span>38<span>]</span></a></sup>
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Wanderlust_(Bj%C3%B6rk_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Wanderlust
(Bj&ouml;rk
song)">Wanderlust</a>&quot;
was
subsequently
released
in
a
similar
format,
featuring
Encyclopedia
Pictura's
short
film
directed
for
the
track,
shot
in
<a
href="/wiki/Stereoscopy?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stereoscopy">stereoscopic</a>
<a
href="/wiki/Three-dimensional_space?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Three-dimensional
space">3D</a>.
The
fifth
single
released
from
the
album
was
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/The_Dull_Flame_of_Desire?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Dull
Flame
of
Desire">The
Dull
Flame
of
Desire</a>&quot;,
featuring
vocals
by
<a
href="/wiki/Antony_Hegarty?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Antony
Hegarty">Antony
Hegarty</a>.</p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
then
completed
an
18-month
world
tour,
having
performed
at
many
festivals
and
returning
to
Latin
America
after
nine
years,
playing
in
<a
href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rio
de
Janeiro">Rio
de
Janeiro</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="S&atilde;o
Paulo">S&atilde;o
Paulo</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Curitiba?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Curitiba">Curitiba</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Guadalajara?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Guadalajara">Guadalajara</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Bogot%C3%A1?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bogot&aacute;">Bogot&aacute;</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Lima?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lima">Lima</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Santiago_de_Chile?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Santiago
de
Chile"
class="mw-redirect">Santiago
de
Chile</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Buenos_Aires?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Buenos
Aires">Buenos
Aires</a>,
as
part
of
different
events.
She
also
returned
to
Australia
and
New
Zealand
for
the
first
time
in
12
years
in
January
2008,
touring
the
nations
with
the
<a
href="/wiki/Big_Day_Out?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Big
Day
Out">Big
Day
Out
Festival</a>.
She
played
a
one-off
show
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/Sydney_Opera_House?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sydney
Opera
House">Sydney
Opera
House</a>
as
part
of
the
<a
href="/wiki/Sydney_Festival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sydney
Festival">Sydney
Festival</a>.
At
a
<a
href="/wiki/Shanghai?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>
performance
she
caused
controversy
by
shouting
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Tibet?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tibet">Tibet</a>!
Tibet!&quot;
at
the
end
of
the
song
&quot;Declare
Independence&quot;.
A
Chinese
official
later
claimed
that

had
hurt
the
feelings
of
the
Chinese
people.<sup
id="cite_ref-39"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-39"><span>[</span>39<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Announced
via
an
<a
href="/wiki/EBay?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="EBay">eBay</a>
<a
href="/wiki/Auction?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Auction">auction</a>,
a
new
Bj&ouml;rk
track
was
revealed
under
the
title
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/N%C3%A1tt%C3%BAra?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="N&aacute;tt&uacute;ra">N&aacute;tt&uacute;ra</a>&quot;.
Bj&ouml;rk
commented
the
song
was
&quot;composed
especially
to
encourage
active
support
for
a
more
environmental
approach
to
Iceland's
natural
resources
than
those
suggested
by
parties
who
are
aloof
and
blind
to
the
consequences
of
their
actions.&quot;<br
/>
The
song
was
initially
labeled
as
a
new
single
by
Bj&ouml;rk,
with
backing
vocals
from
Radiohead
frontman
<a
href="/wiki/Thom_Yorke?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Thom
Yorke">Thom
Yorke</a>.
Bj&ouml;rk's
official
website
later
confirmed
that
the
single
would
be
released
on
October
27,
2008
through
<a
href="/wiki/ITunes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="ITunes">iTunes</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-40"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-40"><span>[</span>40<span>]</span></a></sup>
however
the
track
was
eventually
made
available
at
nattura.grapewire.net,
exclusively.<sup
id="cite_ref-41"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-41"><span>[</span>41<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p><a
href="/wiki/Damian_Taylor?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Damian
Taylor">Damian
Taylor</a>
has
mentioned
collaborating
with
Bj&ouml;rk
on
her
new
album
using
instruments
like
the
<a
href="/wiki/Reactable?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Reactable">Reactable</a>
and
the
<a
href="/wiki/Tenori-on?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tenori-on">Tenori-on</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-42"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-42"><span>[</span>42<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>According
to
an
October
2008
interview
with
<i>Pitchfork</i>
magazine,
Bj&ouml;rk
plans
to
take
the
next
three
to
four
years
to
record
her
next
album.<sup
id="cite_ref-43"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-43"><span>[</span>43<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
a
statement
released
by
bjork.com,
a
limited
edition
box
set
titled
<i><a
href="/wiki/Volta%C3%AFc?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Volta&iuml;c">Volta&iuml;c</a></i>
from
One
Little
Indian
Records
was
announced,
with
a
release
date
in
North
America
of
April
20,
2009</p>

<p>(later
delayed
to
mid-June).
The
release
consists
of
various
live
recordings
of
performances
in
Paris
and
Reykjav&iacute;k.</p>








<p>The
live
set
was
also
recorded
at
the
Olympic
Studio
in
London.
The
release
is
available
as
Standard,
Deluxe,
and
Deluxe
Vinyl,
including
up
to
four
discs,
depending
on
format.
The
first
disc
is
audio
of
songs
from
the
Volta
Tour
performed
live
at
Olympic
Studios;
the
second
disc
contains
video
of
the
Volta
Tour
live
in
Paris
and
live
in
Reykjavik;
the
third
disc
contains
&quot;The
Volta
Videos&quot;
and
the
video
competition,
while
the
fourth
is
<i>The
Volta
Mixes</i>
CD.<sup
id="cite_ref-44"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-44"><span>[</span>44<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
May
2010,
the
<a
href="/wiki/Royal_Swedish_Academy_of_Music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Royal
Swedish
Academy
of
Music">Royal
Swedish
Academy
of
Music</a>
announced
that
Bj&ouml;rk
was
to
receive
the
prestigious
<a
href="/wiki/Polar_Music_Prize?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Polar
Music
Prize">Polar
Music
Prize</a>
alongside
<a
href="/wiki/Ennio_Morricone?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ennio
Morricone">Ennio
Morricone</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-45"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-45"><span>[</span>45<span>]</span></a></sup>
A
month
later,
Bj&ouml;rk,
along
with
<a
href="/wiki/Dirty_Projectors?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"

Projectors">Dirty
Projectors</a>,
announced
that
they
would
be

on
a

<i><a

onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"

Wittenberg
Orca">Mount
Wittenberg
Orca</a></i>,
which
was
released
on
30
June,
to
raise
money
for
marine
conservation.<sup
id="cite_ref-46"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-46"><span>[</span>46<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
September
2010,
Bj&ouml;rk
released
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/The_Comet_Song?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Comet
Song">The
Comet
Song</a>&quot;
as
part
of
the
soundtrack
for
the
movie
<i><a
href="/wiki/Moomins_and_the_Comet_Chase?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Moomins
and
the
Comet
Chase">Moomins
and
the
Comet
Chase</a></i>.
Also
in
2010,
she
dueted
with
fellow
Icelander
(and
<a
href="/wiki/One_Little_Indian?qsrc=3044"

Indian"
class="mw-redirect">One

Indian</a>
labelmate)
<a

onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="&Oacute;l&ouml;f
Arnalds">&Oacute;l&ouml;f
Arnalds</a>
on
a
track
called
&quot;Surrender&quot;
from
Arnalds's
new
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Innundir_skinni?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Innundir
skinni">Innundir
skinni</a></i>,<sup
id="cite_ref-47"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
performed
a
duet
with
<a
href="/wiki/Antony_and_the_Johnsons?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Antony
and
the
Johnsons">Antony
and
the
Johnsons</a>
on
the
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Swanlights?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Swanlights">Swanlights</a></i>.
The
song
is
titled
&quot;Fl&eacute;tta&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-48"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-48"><span>[</span>48<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>On
20
September
2010,
Bj&ouml;rk
performed
her
version
of
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Gloomy_Sunday?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gloomy
Sunday">Gloomy
Sunday</a>&quot;
at
designer
<a
href="/wiki/Alexander_McQueen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Alexander
McQueen">Alexander
McQueen</a>'s
memorial
in
St.
Paul's
cathedral
in
London.
On
7
December
2010,
a
previously
unreleased
song
was
released
by
Bj&ouml;rk
soundtracking
a
film
made
by
Nick
Knight
as
a
tribute
to
McQueen,
with
whom
Bj&ouml;rk
collaborated
on
multiple
occasions.</p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
appeared
on
&Aacute;tta
Raddir,
one
of
J&oacute;nas
Sen's
TV
shows.<sup
id="cite_ref-49"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
episode
aired
on
February
27,
2011.<sup
id="cite_ref-50"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-50"><span>[</span>50<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
shows
are
produced
by
the
Icelandic
National
Broadcasting
Service.<sup
id="cite_ref-51"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
the
show
Bj&ouml;rk
performed
eight
songs,
including
&quot;Sun
in
My
Mouth&quot;,
which
had
not
previously
been
performed
live.</p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="2011.E2.80.93present:_Biophilia.2C_music.2C_technology_and_nature">2011–present:
<i>Biophilia</i>,
music,
technology
and
nature</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a

section:
2011–present:
Biophilia,
music,
technology
and
nature">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<div
class="thumb
tright">









<div

Bj&ouml;rk

Thunderbolt
live

<p>Bj&ouml;rk,
along
with
long-time
collaborative
partner,
Michel
Gondry,
were
originally
announced
to
collaborate
on
a
3-D
&quot;scientific
musical&quot;.
Gondry
states
that
it
will
be
a
40-minute
IMAX
museum
project.<sup
id="cite_ref-52"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
3
December
2010,
in
an
interview
with
Pitchfork,
Bj&ouml;rk
was
asked
if
she
was
&quot;working
on
anything
at
the
moment,&quot;
and
she
replied,
&quot;Yes,
it
will
be
ready
in
[a]
few
months.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-53"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-53"><span>[</span>53<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
17
February
2011,
Pitchfork
reported
that
Bj&ouml;rk
would
release
a
collaboration
with
Syrian
musician
<a
href="/wiki/Omar_Souleyman?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Omar
Souleyman">Omar
Souleyman</a>.
The
project
will
be
available
&quot;on
limited
12-inch,
CD,
and
digital
download
sometime
this
year&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-54"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-54"><span>[</span>54<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>On
17
March
2011,
Bj&ouml;rk
confirmed
details
about
her
next
project,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Biophilia_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Biophilia
(album)">Biophilia</a></i>.
The
new
project
will
combine
music
with
technological
innovation
and
themes
of
science
and
nature,
including
an
&quot;app
album&quot;,
educational
collaborations
with
children
and
specialized
live
performance,
kicking
off
in
<a
href="/wiki/Manchester?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Manchester">Manchester</a>,
United
Kingdom
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/Manchester_International_Festival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Manchester
International
Festival">Manchester
International
Festival</a>
on
30
June.
She
will
perform
at
the
event
for
six
nights.
It
is
expected
that
<i>Biophilia</i>
will
see
her
tour
a
select
number
of
cities
with
extended
residencies.<sup
id="cite_ref-55"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup>
Bj&ouml;rk
performed
at
<a
href="/wiki/Bestival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bestival">Bestival</a>
on
11
September.
The
press
release
stated
that
this
would
be
her
only
outdoor
concert
of
the
year.<sup
id="cite_ref-56"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup>
She
is
also
scheduled
to
perform
six
shows,
two
of
them
during
the
<a
href="/wiki/Iceland_Airwaves?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Iceland
Airwaves">Iceland
Airwaves</a>
Festival,
at
<a
href="/wiki/Harpa_(concert_hall)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Harpa
(concert
hall)">Harpa</a>
in
Iceland
from
12
October
to
7
November.<sup
id="cite_ref-57"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-57"><span>[</span>57<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
June
2011,
the
first
single
from
<i>Biophilia</i>,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Crystalline_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Crystalline
(song)"
class="mw-redirect">Crystalline</a>&quot;,
was
released.<sup
id="cite_ref-58"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-58"><span>[</span>58<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
song
was
composed
using
complex
breakbeats
along
with
only
one
of
several
specialized
instruments
custom
built
for
the
project,
the
&quot;gameleste&quot;,
a
<a
href="/wiki/Celesta?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Celesta">celesta</a>
modified
with
elements
of
<a
href="/wiki/Gamelan?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gamelan">gamelan</a>.
Other
instruments
used
on
the
album
and
in
Bjork's
live
performances
harness
lightning
to
create
sound.</p>








<p>A
central
part
of
<i>Biophilia</i>
is
a
series
of
interactive
<a
href="/wiki/IPad?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="IPad">iPad</a>
apps
made
by
leading
programmers
and
designers,
one
app
for
each
of
the
10
songs
on
the
new
album.
Bjork
discussed
how
the
apps
would
represent
the
scientific
and
natural
ideas
within
the
songs
and
enable
people
to
play
and
understand
the
songs
and
ideas
in
different
ways,
such
as
&quot;Virus&quot;,
a
love
song
between
a
virus
and
a
cell,
in
which
the
&quot;Virus&quot;
app
will
stop
playing
the
song
if
you
are
successful
in
stopping
the
destructive
relationship.
Two
of
the
apps,
&quot;Crystalline&quot;
and
&quot;Cosmogony&quot;,
were
released
on
19
July
2011,
along
with
a
music
video
for
&quot;Crystalline&quot;,
directed
by
Michel
Gondry.
However,
the
album
was
released
in
usual
form
as
a
series
of
10
music
tracks
as
well,
including
a
CD
release,
on
10
October
2011,
and
Bjork
said
it
is
designed
to
work
as
music
just
as
any
of
her
other
albums
is.</p>








<p>In
a
June
2011
interview
with
<a
href="/wiki/Stereogum?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stereogum">Stereogum</a>,
Bj&ouml;rk
stated
that
her
contract
with
her
international
record
labels
(excluding
One
Little
Indian,
UK)
had
ended
since
all
promotions
for
<i>Volta</i>
concluded
and
that
she
has
signed
with
both
<a
href="/wiki/National_Geographic_Society?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="National
Geographic
Society">National
Geographic</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Nonesuch_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nonesuch
Records">Nonesuch</a>
for
<i>Biophilia</i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-59"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-59"><span>[</span>59<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-60"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-60"><span>[</span>60<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Artistry">Artistry</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9"
title="Edit
section:
Artistry">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Compositions">Compositions</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10"
title="Edit
section:
Compositions">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk's
music
style
tends
to
be
quite
eclectic
and
often
challenging.
She
has
embraced
many
genres
throughout
her
career,
creating
a
varied
range
of
pieces,
from
<a
href="/wiki/Big_band_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Big
band
music"
class="mw-redirect">big
band
music</a>
to
<a
href="/wiki/Art_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Art
music">sound
art</a>.
Bj&ouml;rk's
lyrical
themes
range
from
personal
matters
to
scientific,
environmentalist,
or
social
topics.</p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Voice">Voice</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11"
title="Edit
section:
Voice">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
possesses
a
<a
href="/wiki/Soprano?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Soprano">soprano</a>
vocal
range,<sup
id="cite_ref-61"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-61"><span>[</span>61<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-62"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-62"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup>
which
has
been
described
as
both
&quot;elastic&quot;
and
&quot;somersaulting&quot;
in
quality
as
well
as
having
been
praised
for
her
<a
href="/wiki/Scat_singing?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Scat
singing">scatting</a>
ability,
unique
vocal
stylings
and
delivery.<sup
id="cite_ref-63"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-63"><span>[</span>63<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
a
review
for
her
live
performance
at
the
2011
<a
href="/wiki/Manchester_International_Festival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Manchester
International
Festival">Manchester
International
Festival</a>
Bernadette
McNulty
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Daily
Telegraph">The
Daily
Telegraph</a></i>
commented
on
her
voice
and
music,
&quot;the
45-year-old
still
uses
electronic
dance
beats
with
a
full-blooded
raver’s
passion
and
the
elemental
<a
href="/wiki/Timbre?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Timbre">timbre</a>
of
her
voice
has
grown
more
powerful
with
age&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-64"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-64"><span>[</span>64<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
late
2012
it
was
reported
that
Bj&ouml;rk
had
undergone
surgery
for
a
polyp
on
her
vocal
cords,
commenting
on
the
success
of
the
procedure
after
years
of
maintaining
a
strict
diet
and
utilising
vocal
exercises
to
prevent
vocal
injury
she
stated,
&quot;I
have
to
say,
in
my
case
anyway:
surgery
rocks!&quot;
continuing
on
&quot;I
stayed
quiet
for
three
weeks
and
then
started
singing
and
definitely
feel
like
my
cords
are
as
good
as
pre-<a
href="/wiki/Vocal_nodules?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Vocal
nodules"
class="mw-redirect">nodule</a>,
it's
been
very
satisfying
to
sing
all
them
clear
notes
again.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-65"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-65"><span>[</span>65<span>]</span></a></sup>
However
in
a
review
for
<i>Biophilia</i>
<a
href="/wiki/Kitty_Empire?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kitty
Empire">Kitty
Empire</a>
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Guardian?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Guardian">The
Guardian</a></i>
stated
that
pre-surgery
Bj&ouml;rk
still
sounded
strong
commenting
that
her
voice
was
&quot;spectacular
and
swooping&quot;,
particularly
on
the
song
&quot;Thunderbolt&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-66"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-66"><span>[</span>66<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
a
similar
vein
Matthew
Cole
of
<a
href="/wiki/Slant_Magazine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Slant
Magazine">Slant
Magazine</a>
adds
that
her
voice
has
been
&quot;preserved
quite
well&quot;
however
he
also
stipulates
that
&quot;her
once-formidable
wail
is
too
hoarse
and
shouty
to
be
the
ace
in
the
hole
that
it
once
was&quot;
also
adding
&quot;it's
only
where
her
most
dramatic
vocal
pyrotechnics
are
concerned
that
there's
any
question
of
physical
ability&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-67"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-67"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/NPR?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="NPR">National
Public
Radio</a>
counted
Bj&ouml;rk
among
its
list
of
&quot;50
Great
Voices&quot;
and
MTV
placed
her
at
number
8
on
its
countdown
&quot;22
Greatest
Voices
in
Music&quot;
she
also
placed
60/100
as
one
of
the
greatest
singers
ever
by
<i><a
href="/wiki/Rolling_Stone?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rolling
Stone">Rolling
Stone</a></i>
who
praised
her
voice
as
being
unique,
fresh
and
extremely
versatile,
fitting
and
being
influenced
by
a
wide
range
of
influences
and
genres.<sup
id="cite_ref-MTV_voices_8-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-MTV_voices-8"><span>[</span>8<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-Rolling_Stone_voices_9-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Rolling_Stone_voices-9"><span>[</span>9<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<p>Bj&ouml;rk's
intermittent
acting
career
began
in
1986,
when
she
appeared
in
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Juniper_Tree_(film)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Juniper
Tree
(film)">The
Juniper
Tree</a></i>,
a
tale
of
<a
href="/wiki/Witchcraft?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Witchcraft">witchcraft</a>
based
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/Brothers_Grimm?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Brothers
Grimm">Brothers
Grimm</a>
story
of
the
same
name.
Bj&ouml;rk
played
the
role
of
Margit,
a
girl
whose
mother
has
been
killed
for
practicing
witchcraft.
Bj&ouml;rk
also
had
an
uncredited
role
in
1994's
<i><a
href="/wiki/Pr%C3%AAt-%C3%A0-Porter_(film)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pr&ecirc;t-&agrave;-Porter
(film)">Pr&ecirc;t-&agrave;-Porter</a></i>.</p>








<p>In
1999,
Bj&ouml;rk
was
asked
to
write
and
produce
the
musical
score
for
the
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/Dancer_in_the_Dark?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dancer
in
the
Dark">Dancer
in
the
Dark</a></i>,
a
musical
drama
about
an
immigrant
named
Selma
who
is
struggling
to
pay
for
an
operation
to
prevent
her
son
from
going
blind.
Director
<a
href="/wiki/Lars_von_Trier?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lars
von
Trier">Lars
von
Trier</a>
eventually
asked
her
to
consider
playing
the
role
of
Selma,
convincing
her
that
the
only
true
way
to
capture
the
character
of
Selma
was
to
have
the
composer
of
the
music
play
the
character.<sup
id="cite_ref-68"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-68"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup>
Eventually,
she
accepted.
Filming
began
in
early
1999,
and
the
film
debuted
in
2000
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/2000_Cannes_Film_Festival?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="2000
Cannes
Film
Festival">53rd
Cannes
Film
Festival</a>.
The
film
received
the
<a
href="/wiki/Palme_d%27Or?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Palme
d'Or">Palme
d'Or</a>,
and
Bj&ouml;rk
received
the
<a
href="/wiki/Best_Actress_Award_(Cannes_Film_Festival)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Best
Actress
Award
(Cannes
Film
Festival)">Best
Actress
Award</a>
for
her
role.<sup
id="cite_ref-festival-cannes.com_6-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-festival-cannes.com-6"><span>[</span>6<span>]</span></a></sup>
It
was
reported
that
the
shoot
was
so
physically
and
emotionally
tiring
that
she
vowed
never
to
act
again.
Bj&ouml;rk
later
stated
that
she
always
wanted
to
do
one
musical
in
her
life,
and
this
was
the
one.<sup
id="cite_ref-69"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-69"><span>[</span>69<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>The
soundtrack
Bj&ouml;rk
created
for
the
film
was
released
with
the
title
<i><a
href="/wiki/Selmasongs?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Selmasongs"
class="mw-redirect">Selmasongs</a></i>.
The
album
features
a
duet
with
<a
href="/wiki/Thom_Yorke?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Thom
Yorke">Thom
Yorke</a>
of
<a
href="/wiki/Radiohead?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Radiohead">Radiohead</a>
titled
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/I%27ve_Seen_It_All?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="I've
Seen
It
All">I've
Seen
It
All</a>&quot;,
which
was
nominated
for
an
<a
href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Original_Song?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Academy
Award
for
Best
Original
Song">Academy
Award
for
Best
Song</a>
and
was
performed
at
the
2001
Oscars,
while
Bj&ouml;rk
was
wearing
her
celebrated<sup
id="cite_ref-70"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-70"><span>[</span>70<span>]</span></a></sup>
&quot;swan
dress&quot;,
a
copy
of
which
was
auctioned
off
for
international
aid
agency
<a
href="/wiki/Oxfam?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Oxfam">Oxfam</a>
on
<a
href="/wiki/EBay?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="EBay">eBay</a>
and
sold
for
$9,500
in
2005.<sup
id="cite_ref-abc_swan_dress_1_71-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-abc_swan_dress_1-71"><span>[</span>71<span>]</span></a></sup>
She
was
invited
to
record
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Gollum%27s_Song?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gollum's
Song"
class="mw-redirect">Gollum's
Song</a>&quot;
for
the
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Lord_of_the_Rings:_The_Two_Towers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Lord
of
the
Rings:
The
Two
Towers">The
Lord
of
the
Rings:
The
Two
Towers</a></i>
but
declined
the
invitation,
as
she
was
then
pregnant;
the
song
was
instead
recorded
by
another
Icelander,
<a
href="/wiki/Emil%C3%ADana_Torrini?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Emil&iacute;ana
Torrini">Emil&iacute;ana
Torrini</a>.</p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
starred
in
Gunar
Karlsson's
2007
animated
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/Anna_and_the_Moods?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Anna
and
the
Moods">Anna
and
the
Moods</a></i>,
along
with
<a
href="/wiki/Terry_Jones?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Terry
Jones">Terry
Jones</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Damon_Albarn?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Damon
Albarn">Damon
Albarn</a>.
Bj&ouml;rk
also
appeared
in
the
2005
documentary
<i><a
href="/wiki/Screaming_Masterpiece?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Screaming
Masterpiece">Screaming
Masterpiece</a></i>,
which
delves
into
the
Icelandic
music
scene.
The
movie
features
archive
footage
of
<a
href="/wiki/The_Sugarcubes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Sugarcubes">the
Sugarcubes</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Tappi_T%C3%ADkarrass?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tappi
T&iacute;karrass">Tappi
T&iacute;karrass</a>
and
an
ongoing
conversation
with
Bj&ouml;rk
herself.</p>








<p>Her
partner
<a
href="/wiki/Matthew_Barney?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Matthew
Barney">Matthew
Barney</a>
is
a
contemporary
artist
based
in
New
York.
Bj&ouml;rk
collaborated
with
him
on
the
experimental
art
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/Drawing_Restraint_9?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Drawing
Restraint
9">Drawing
Restraint
9</a></i>,
a
dialogueless
exploration
of
<a
href="/wiki/Culture_of_Japan?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Culture
of
Japan">Japanese
culture</a>.
Bj&ouml;rk
and
Barney
both
appear
in
the
film,
which
was
released
in
2005.
She
is
also
responsible
for
the
film's
soundtrack,
her
second
after
<i>Selmasongs</i>.</p>








<p>Director
and
previous
collaborator
<a
href="/wiki/Michel_Gondry?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Michel
Gondry">Michel
Gondry</a>
asked
Bj&ouml;rk
to
star
in
his
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Science_of_Sleep?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Science
of
Sleep">The
Science
of
Sleep</a></i>,
but
she
declined.
The
role
was
played
by
<a
href="/wiki/Charlotte_Gainsbourg?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Charlotte
Gainsbourg">Charlotte
Gainsbourg</a>
instead.<sup
id="cite_ref-72"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-72"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>She
collaborated
with
<a
href="/wiki/SHOWstudio?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="SHOWstudio"
class="mw-redirect">SHOWstudio</a>
and
founder
<a
href="/wiki/Nick_Knight_(photographer)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nick
Knight
(photographer)">Nick
Knight</a>
in
2010
by
providing
music
for
an
<a
href="/wiki/Alexander_McQueen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Alexander
McQueen">Alexander
McQueen</a>
tribute.</p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk's
single
&quot;Declare
Independence&quot;
was
used
in
the
<a
rel="nofollow"
class="external
text"
href="http://vimeo.com/53619913">trailer
for
the

of

<p>In
July
2013,
she
featured
in
a
<a
href="/wiki/Channel_4?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Channel
4">Channel
4</a>
documentary
programme
along
with
Sir
<a
href="/wiki/David_Attenborough?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="David
Attenborough">David
Attenborough</a>
called
<i>When
Bj&ouml;rk
Met
Attenborough</i>,
as
part
of
their
<i>Mad4Music</i>
season
of
programmes,
in
which
each
episode
features
musicians
from
across
the
musical
spectrum
giving
an
alternative
take
on
music
and
what
it
means
to
them
and
others
around
them,
for
example
the
first
episode
featured
pianist
<a
href="/wiki/James_Rhodes_(pianist)?qsrc=3044"

Rhodes
(pianist)">James
Rhodes</a>.

and

with

around

<i><a
href="/wiki/Biophilia_(album)?qsrc=3044"

title="Biophilia
(album)">Biophilia</a></i>,
and

featured
scientist
<a
href="/wiki/Oliver_Sacks?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"

class="reference"><a

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Charitable_work">Charitable
work</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13"
title="Edit
section:
Charitable
work">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>After
the
<a
href="/wiki/2004_Indian_Ocean_earthquake_and_tsunami?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="2004
Indian
Ocean
earthquake
and
tsunami">tsunami</a>
which
struck
<a
href="/wiki/Southeast_Asia?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Southeast
Asia">Southeast
Asia</a>
in
late
2004,
Bj&ouml;rk
began
work
on
a
new
project
titled
<i><a
href="/wiki/Army_of_Me:_Remixes_and_Covers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Army
of
Me:
Remixes
and
Covers">Army
of
Me:
Remixes
and
Covers</a></i>
to
help
raise
money
for
a
relief
fund.
This
project
recruited
fans
and
musicians
from
around
the
world
to
either
cover
or
remix
the
1995
track,
&quot;Army
of
Me&quot;.
From
over
600
responses
Bj&ouml;rk
and
her
co-writer
Graham
Massey
picked
the
best
twenty
to
appear
on
the
album.
The
album
was
released
in
April
in
the
UK
and
in
late
May
2005
in
the
US.
By
January
2006,
the
album
had
raised
around
&pound;250,000
to
help
<a
href="/wiki/UNICEF?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a>'s
work
in
the
southeast
Asian
region.<sup
id="cite_ref-74"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-74"><span>[</span>74<span>]</span></a></sup>
Bj&ouml;rk
visited
<a
href="/wiki/Banda_Aceh?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Banda
Aceh">Banda
Aceh</a>
in
February
2006
to
view
some
of
<a
href="/wiki/UNICEF?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a>'s
work
with
the
children
who
were
affected
by
the
tsunami.<sup
id="cite_ref-75"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-75"><span>[</span>75<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>On
2
July
2005
Bj&ouml;rk
took
part
in
the
historic
<a
href="/wiki/Live_8?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Live
8">Live
8</a>
series
of
concerts,
headlining
the
<a
href="/wiki/Live_8_concert,_Chiba?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Live
8
concert,
Chiba">Japan
show</a>
with
<a
href="/wiki/Do_As_Infinity?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Do
As
Infinity">Do
As
Infinity</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Good_Charlotte?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Good
Charlotte">Good
Charlotte</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/McFly?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="McFly">McFly</a>.
She
performed
eight
songs
with
<a
href="/wiki/Matmos?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Matmos">Matmos</a>,
a
<a
href="/wiki/Japan?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Japan">Japanese</a>
<a
href="/wiki/String_instrument?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="String
instrument">string</a>
<a
href="/wiki/Octet_(music)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Octet
(music)">octet</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Zeena_Parkins?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Zeena
Parkins">Zeena
Parkins</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-76"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-76"><span>[</span>76<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
has
also
taken
an
interest
in
environmental
issues
in
her
native
country.
In
2004,
Bj&ouml;rk
took
part
in
the
&quot;H&aelig;tta&quot;
concert
in
Reykjav&iacute;k,
organised
in
protest
against
the
building
of
<a
href="/wiki/Alcoa?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Alcoa">Alcoa</a>
<a
href="/wiki/Aluminium?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Aluminium">aluminium</a>
smelters
in
the
country,
which
would
make
Iceland
the
biggest
smelter
in
Europe.
She
founded
the
organization
&quot;N&aacute;tt&uacute;ra&quot;,
which
aims
to
promote
Icelandic
nature
and
grassroots
industries.
On
October
28,
2008,
Bj&ouml;rk
wrote
an
article
for
the
Times
discussing
the
state
of
the
Icelandic
economy
and
her
thoughts
on
the
proposed
use
of
natural
resources
to
get
the
country
out
of
debt.
Bj&ouml;rk,
in
collaboration
with
<a
href="/wiki/Audur_Capital?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Audur
Capital">Audur
Capital</a>,
set
up
a
venture
capital
fund
titled
&quot;BJ&Ouml;RK&quot;
to
support
the
creation
of
sustainable
industries
in
Iceland.
She
has
written
the
foreword
to
the
English
translation
of
the
Iceland
bestseller
by
<a
href="/wiki/Andri_Sn%C3%A6r_Magnason?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Andri
Sn&aelig;r
Magnason">Andri
Sn&aelig;r
Magnason</a>
titled
&quot;Dreamland&quot;.</p>








<p>On
May
21,
2010,
Bj&ouml;rk
wrote
an
open
letter
in
the
newspaper
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Reykjav%C3%ADk_Grapevine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Reykjav&iacute;k
Grapevine">The
Reykjav&iacute;k
Grapevine</a></i>,
calling
on
the
Icelandic
government
to
&quot;do
everything
in
its
power
to
revoke
the
contracts
with
<a
href="/wiki/Magma_Energy?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Magma
Energy"
class="mw-redirect">Magma
Energy</a>&quot;,
the
Canadian
company
which
now
has
complete
ownership
of
Icelandic
geothermal
company
HS
Orka.<sup
id="cite_ref-77"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-77"><span>[</span>77<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Prot.C3.A9g.C3.A9s">Prot&eacute;g&eacute;s</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14"
title="Edit
section:
Prot&eacute;g&eacute;s">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Over
her
extensive
career,
Bj&ouml;rk
has
frequently
used
her
position
and
influence
to
help
launch
new
acts
or
<a
href="/wiki/Mentor?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mentor">mentor</a>
them
as
they
establish
themselves
as
recording
artists.</p>








<p>The
first
example
of
this
was
most
evident
with
Iranian-born
<a
href="/wiki/Electronica?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electronica">electronica</a>
producer
<a
href="/wiki/Leila_Arab?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Leila
Arab">Leila
Arab</a>.
Leila
was
initially
recruited
to
play
<a
href="/wiki/Keyboard_instrument?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Keyboard
instrument">keyboards</a>
and
provide
backing
vocals
on
Bj&ouml;rk's
first
international
solo
tour
in
1993
in
support
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Debut_(Bj%C3%B6rk_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Debut
(Bj&ouml;rk
album)">Debut</a></i>.
In
1995,
Bj&ouml;rk
recalled
Leila
to
be
part
of
her
second
touring
band
for
her
next
tour
in
support
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Post_(Bj%C3%B6rk_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Post
(Bj&ouml;rk
album)">Post</a></i>.
This
time
Leila
was
given
the
opportunity
to
experiment
with
the
live
output
mixing
from
the
stage,
rather
than
playing
keyboards.
This
was
to
be
Leila's
first
encounter
with
live
mixing
and
would
later
form
the
basis
of
her
own
solo
music
career
where
she
has
integrated
live
mixing
into
her
own
compositions
and
live
shows.
Leila
has
gone
on
to
release
three
international
solo
albums
throughout
the
1990s
and
appears
on
the
influential
<a
href="/wiki/Electronica?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electronica">electronica</a>
labels
<a
href="/wiki/Rephlex_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rephlex
Records">Rephlex
Records</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/XL_Recordings?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="XL
Recordings">XL
Recordings</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Warp_(record_label)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Warp
(record
label)">Warp
Records</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-78"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-78"><span>[</span>78<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
1998,
Bj&ouml;rk
established
her
own
short-lived
record
label,
Ear
Records,
which
operated
under
the
<a
href="/wiki/One_Little_Indian_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="One
Little
Indian
Records">One
Little
Indian
Records</a>
umbrella.
Her
only
signee
that
received
a
release
was
her
long-time
friend,
Magga
St&iacute;na.
Magga
St&iacute;na
recorded
her
debut
solo
album
under
the
production
of
Bj&ouml;rk's
longtime
collaborator,
<a
href="/wiki/Graham_Massey?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Graham
Massey">Graham
Massey</a>
(of
the
British
electronica
act
<a
href="/wiki/808_State?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="808
State">808
State</a>.)
The
album
was
simply
titled
<i>An
Album</i>
and
featured
just
one
single
release,
&quot;Naturally&quot;.
In
1998,
Bj&ouml;rk
invited
Magga
St&iacute;na
to
perform
as
her
support
act
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/List_of_Bj%C3%B6rk_concert_tours?qsrc=3044#Homogenic_Tour"
title="List
of
Bj&ouml;rk
concert
tours">Homogenic
world
tour</a>,
and
in
2004
St&iacute;na
contributed
to
the
production
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Med%C3%BAlla?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Med&uacute;lla">Med&uacute;lla</a></i>.
St&iacute;na
is
presently
still
performing
and
recording
in
Iceland.</p>








<p>In
2001,
Bj&ouml;rk
heard
of
a
Canadian
<a
href="/wiki/Inuit_throat_singing?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Inuit
throat
singing">Inuit
throat
singer</a>
named
<a
href="/wiki/Tagaq?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tagaq">Tagaq</a>
and
invited
her
to
perform
on
several
dates
of
Bj&ouml;rk's
<a
href="/wiki/List_of_Bj%C3%B6rk_concert_tours?qsrc=3044#Vespertine_Tour"
title="List
of
Bj&ouml;rk
concert
tours">Vespertine
world
tour</a>
as
a
special
guest.
In
2004,
Tagaq
was
invited
to
collaborate
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/A_cappella?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="A
cappella">a
cappella</a>
album,
<i>Med&uacute;lla</i>,
in
which
the
duet
&quot;Ancestors&quot;
was
recorded.
&quot;Ancestors&quot;
was
later
featured
on
Tagaq's
first
solo
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Sinaa?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sinaa">Sinaa</a></i>,
in
2005.</p>








<p>In
2004,
Leila
discovered
the
work
of
Finnish
multimedia
artist
Heidi
Kilpel&auml;inen,
who
had
taken
her
combination
of
<a
href="/wiki/Low_fidelity?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Low
fidelity">Lo-fi</a>,
homemade
<a
href="/wiki/Electro_(music)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electro
(music)">electro</a>
pop
with
her
own
self-produced
<a
href="/wiki/Music_videos?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Music
videos"
class="mw-redirect">music
videos</a>
and
combined
them
under
the
<a
href="/wiki/Alter_ego?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Alter
ego">alter
ego</a>
character,
<a
href="/wiki/HK119?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="HK119">HK119</a>.
Leila
soon
referred
HK119's
work
to
Bj&ouml;rk,
who
quickly
and
excitedly
started
mentioning
HK119
in
various
press
and
interviews.
In
2004,
Bj&ouml;rk
announced
HK119
as
her
favourite
act
of
2004
and
cited
her
as
&quot;The
Perfect
Blonde
Woman&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-79"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-79"><span>[</span>79<span>]</span></a></sup>
HK119
was
soon
signed
to
Bj&ouml;rk's
parent
label
One
Little
Indian
Records,
which
released
her
<a
href="/wiki/HK119_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="HK119
(album)">debut
album</a>
in
2006.
HK119
and
Bj&ouml;rk
appeared
in
a
joint
interview
in
Dazed
&amp;
Confused
magazine
in
2006,
where
Bj&ouml;rk
stated
about
HK119's
work,
&quot;It's
unique.
Even
if
I
gave
you
$3
million,
you
couldn't
improve
on
it...
[Its]
simplicity
is
[its]
strength.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-80"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-80"><span>[</span>80<span>]</span></a></sup>
HK119
later
released
her
albums,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Fast,_Cheap_and_Out_of_Control_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Fast,
Cheap
and
Out
of
Control
(album)">Fast,
Cheap
and
Out
of
Control</a></i>
in
2008
and
<i><a
href="/wiki/Imaginature?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Imaginature">Imaginature</a></i>
in
2013,
both
on
One
Little
Indian
Records.</p>








<p>In
2009,
Bj&ouml;rk
used
her
website
and
various
radio
interviews
throughout
the
year
to
express
her
enthusiasm
for
two
more
new
acts.
The
first
was
fellow
Icelandic
musician,
<a
href="/wiki/%C3%93l%C3%B6f_Arnalds?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="&Oacute;l&ouml;f
Arnalds">&Oacute;l&ouml;f
Arnalds</a>,
who
is
also
a
member
of
Icelandic
<a
href="/wiki/Folktronica?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Folktronica">folktronica</a>
band
<a
href="/wiki/M%C3%BAm?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="M&uacute;m">m&uacute;m</a>.
In
2006,
Arnalds
released
her
debut
solo
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Vi%C3%B0_Og_Vi%C3%B0?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Vi&eth;
Og
Vi&eth;">Vi&eth;
Og
Vi&eth;</a></i>
in
Iceland,
which
Bj&ouml;rk
citied
as
one
of
her
favourite
recent
new
acts
of
the
last
few
years
during
a
radio
interview,
and
encouraged
One
Little
Indian
Records
to
reissue
the
album
in
the
UK
and
Europe
in
2009.
On
the
same
radio
show
for
the
American
NPR
channel,
Bj&ouml;rk
also
praised
the
works
of
emerging
British
artist
<a
href="/wiki/Micachu?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Micachu">Micachu</a>
and
the
more
obscure,
<a
href="/wiki/Omar_Souleyman?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Omar
Souleyman">Omar
Souleyman</a>.
Bj&ouml;rk
later
used
her
official
website
to
host
the
premier
of
<a
href="/wiki/Micachu?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Micachu">Micachu</a>'s
debut
video
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/Rough_Trade_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rough
Trade
Records">Rough
Trade
Records</a>,
&quot;Turn
Me
Well&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-81"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-81"><span>[</span>81<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Personal_life">Personal
life</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15"
title="Edit
section:
Personal
life">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Family">Family</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16"
title="Edit
section:
Family">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk's
father,
<a
href="/wiki/Gu%C3%B0mundur_Gunnarsson?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gu&eth;mundur
Gunnarsson">Gu&eth;mundur
Gunnarsson</a>,
is
a
well
known
<a
href="/wiki/Trade_union?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Trade
union">union</a>
leader
in
Iceland
and
was
nationally
recognized
before
his
daughter
became
famous.
Her
mother,
Hildur
R&uacute;na
Hauksd&oacute;ttir,
has
also
been
politically
active.</p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
has
a
son,
Sindri
Eldon
Th&oacute;rsson,
born
8
June
1986,
with
Th&oacute;r
Eldon,
who
was
her
band
mate
in
the
Sugarcubes.
Sindri
is
a
<a
href="/wiki/Journalism?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Journalism">journalist</a>
and
has
his
own
solo
project
simply
called
&quot;Sindri
Eldon&quot;.</p>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
and
her
partner,
artist
<a
href="/wiki/Matthew_Barney?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Matthew
Barney">Matthew
Barney</a>,
have
a
daughter,
&Iacute;sad&oacute;ra
Bjarkard&oacute;ttir
Barney,
born
3
October
2002.</p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Paparazzi_and_controversy">Paparazzi
and
controversy</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17"
title="Edit
section:
Paparazzi
and
controversy">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
has
complained
of
being
hounded
by
<a
href="/wiki/Paparazzi?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Paparazzi">paparazzi</a>.
In
1996,
Bj&ouml;rk
arrived
at
<a
href="/wiki/Don_Mueang_International_Airport?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Don
Mueang
International
Airport">Bangkok
International
Airport</a>
with
her
son
Sindri
after
a
long
haul
flight
when
Julie
Kaufman,
a
female
reporter,
greeted
Bj&ouml;rk
with
&quot;Welcome
to
Bangkok&quot;,
which
was
then
followed
by
Bj&ouml;rk's
attacking
her
and
knocking
her
to
the
ground.
Bj&ouml;rk
has
said
that
the
reason
for
the
attack
was
that
the
reporters
in
the
airport
started
talking
to
her
son,
saying
such
things
as,
&quot;It
must
be
hard
to
be
the
son
of
a
pop
star.&quot;
Bj&ouml;rk's
record
company
also
said
that
the
reporter
had
been
pestering
Bj&ouml;rk
for
four
days.
Bj&ouml;rk
later
apologized
to
Kaufman,
who
declined
to
involve
the
police.
The
incident
would
appear
on
the
<a
href="/wiki/TruTV?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="TruTV">TruTV</a>
series
<i><a
href="/wiki/TruTV_Presents:_World%27s_Dumbest...?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="TruTV
Presents:
World's
Dumbest...">TruTV
Presents:
World's
Dumbest...</a></i>.</p>








<p>On
13
January
2008,
Bj&ouml;rk
attacked
a
photographer
who
had
photographed
her
arrival
at
<a
href="/wiki/Auckland_International_Airport?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Auckland
International
Airport"
class="mw-redirect">Auckland
International
Airport</a>
in
New
Zealand
for
her
scheduled
performance
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/Big_Day_Out?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Big
Day
Out">Big
Day
Out</a>
festival.<sup
id="cite_ref-82"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-82"><span>[</span>82<span>]</span></a></sup>
Bj&ouml;rk
allegedly
tore
the
photographer's
shirt
down
the
back,
and
in
the
process
she
fell
to
the
ground.<sup
id="cite_ref-3_News_43421_83-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-3_News_43421-83"><span>[</span>83<span>]</span></a></sup>
Neither
the
photographer
nor
his
employer,
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_New_Zealand_Herald?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
New
Zealand
Herald">The
New
Zealand
Herald</a></i>,
lodged
a
formal
complaint,
and
Auckland
police
did
not
investigate
further.<sup
id="cite_ref-NZ_Herald_10486789_84-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-NZ_Herald_10486789-84"><span>[</span>84<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Political_views">Political
views</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18"
title="Edit
section:
Political
views">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk's
years
in
<span
lang="is"
xml:lang="is">Kukl</span>
aligned
her
with
the
<a
href="/wiki/Anarchist?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Anarchist"
class="mw-redirect">anarchist</a>
<a
href="/wiki/Crass_Collective?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Crass
Collective"
class="mw-redirect">Crass
Collective</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-85"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-85"><span>[</span>85<span>]</span></a></sup>
While
she
has
since
been
hesitant
to
be
seen
as
an
overtly
political
figure,
and
has
said
so
on
her
website,<sup
id="cite_ref-cmomse_86-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-cmomse-86"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup>
she
is
strongly
supportive
of
numerous
<a
href="/wiki/Liberation_movement?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Liberation
movement">liberation
movements</a>
across
the
globe,
including
support
for
<a
href="/wiki/Separatism?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Separatism">independence</a>
for
<a
href="/wiki/Kosovo?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-87"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-87"><span>[</span>87<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>She
dedicated
her
song
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Declare_Independence?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Declare
Independence">Declare
Independence</a>&quot;
to
<a
href="/wiki/Greenland?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Greenland">Greenland</a>
and
the
<a
href="/wiki/Faroe_Islands?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Faroe
Islands">Faroe
Islands</a>,
which
caused
a
minor
controversy
in
the
Faroes.
When
Bj&ouml;rk
twice
dedicated
&quot;Declare
Independence&quot;
to
the
people
of
<a
href="/wiki/Kosovo?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>
during
a
concert
in
Japan,<sup
id="cite_ref-88"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-88"><span>[</span>88<span>]</span></a></sup>
a
planned
performance
of
hers
was
cancelled
at
<a
href="/wiki/Serbia?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Serbia">Serbia</a>'s
<a
href="/wiki/Exit_(festival)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Exit
(festival)">Exit
Festival</a>,
reportedly
due
to
safety
concerns.</p>








<p>In
2008,
Bj&ouml;rk
set
off
an
international
controversy
after
she
dedicated
&quot;Declare
Independence&quot;
to
the
<a
href="/wiki/International_Tibet_Independence_Movement?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="International
Tibet
Independence
Movement">Tibet
freedom
movement</a>
during
a
<a
href="/wiki/Shanghai?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a>
concert,
chanting
&quot;Tibet!
Tibet!&quot;
during
the
song.
China's
Culture
Ministry
issued
a
denunciation
through
state
news
agency
<a
href="/wiki/Xinhua_News_Agency?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Xinhua
News
Agency">Xinhua</a>,
stating
that
Bj&ouml;rk
&quot;broke
Chinese
law&quot;
and
&quot;hurt
Chinese
people's
feelings&quot;
and
pledged
to
further
tighten
control
over
foreign
artists
performing
in
China.
A
later
statement
accused
Bj&ouml;rk
of
&quot;whipping
up
ethnic
hatred&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-89"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Sexuality">Sexuality</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19"
title="Edit
section:
Sexuality">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>In
an
interview
with
<i><a
href="/wiki/Diva_(magazine)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Diva
(magazine)">Diva</a></i>
magazine
in
October
2004,
she
said:</p>








<blockquote
class="toccolours"
style="float:none;
padding:
10px
15px
10px
15px;
display:table;">









<p>I
think
everyone's
<a
href="/wiki/Bisexuality?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bisexuality">bisexual</a>
to
some
degree
or
another;
it's
just
a
question
of
whether
or
not
you
choose
to
recognize
it
and
embrace
it.
Personally,
I
think
choosing
between
men
and
women
is
like
choosing
between
cake
and
ice
cream.
You'd
be
daft
not
to
try
both
when
there
are
so
many
different
flavors.<sup
id="cite_ref-90"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-90"><span>[</span>90<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








</blockquote>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
has
accumulated
a
large
gay
<a
href="/wiki/Fandom?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Fandom">fanbase</a>
over
the
years;
in
an
interview
with
<i><a
href="/wiki/Instinct_(magazine)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Instinct
(magazine)">Instinct</a></i>
magazine
in
2004,
she
acknowledged
it,
saying:</p>








<blockquote
class="toccolours"
style="float:none;
padding:
10px
15px
10px
15px;
display:table;">









<p>I
like
to
think
of
people
who
buy
my
records
as
equals.
Don't
think
of
them
as
gay
or
black
or
young
or
old.
They're
just
people
who
enjoy
my
music.
I've
had
so
many
close
gay
friends
all
my
life,
it's
not
that
big
of
a
deal
with
me.
But
I'd
be
lying
if
I
said
there
weren't
things
I
find
easier
to
talk
about
with
gay
guys.<sup
id="cite_ref-91"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-91"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








</blockquote>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Stalker">Stalker</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20"
title="Edit
section:
Stalker">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<div
class="rellink
relarticle
mainarticle">








Main
article:









<a
href="/wiki/Ricardo_Lopez_(stalker)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ricardo
Lopez
(stalker)"
class="mw-redirect">Ricardo
Lopez
(stalker)</a>







</div>








<p>On
12
September
1996,
obsessed
fan
Ricardo
L&oacute;pez
mailed
an
acid-spraying
<a
href="/wiki/Letter_bomb?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Letter
bomb">letter
bomb</a>
to
Bj&ouml;rk's
London
home
and
then
killed
himself,
but
the
package
was
intercepted
by
the
<a
href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Police_Service?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Metropolitan
Police
Service">Metropolitan
Police
Service</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-92"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-92"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup>
L&oacute;pez
filmed
himself
in
the
process
of
making
the
acid
bomb
which
was
intended
to
severely
scar
the
singer's
face
and
torso.
The
nearly
18
hours
of
videotape
described
L&oacute;pez's
obsession
with
Bj&ouml;rk,
the
construction
of
the
device,
his
thoughts
on
love
and
other
subjects,
including
racial
remarks
against
Bj&ouml;rk's
then-boyfriend
<a
href="/wiki/Goldie?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Goldie">Goldie</a>.
The
video
footage
continues
after
his
mailing
the
bomb
to
Bj&ouml;rk's
London
home
and
ends
as
L&oacute;pez
shaves
his
head,
applies
face
paint,
and
commits
suicide
by
shooting
himself
on
camera.<sup
id="cite_ref-93"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-93"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
her
few
public
comments
on
this
event,
Bj&ouml;rk
later
said
it
was
hard
emotionally
and
it
disrupted
her
life
and
work
in
London,
explaining
in
part
why
she
chose
to
leave
the
UK
scene
for
good,
reject
her
cute
image,
and
begin
to
write
more
personally
with
<i>Homogenic</i>
(1997).</p>

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Awards_and_nominations">Awards
and
nominations</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Bj%C3%B6rk&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22"
title="Edit
section:
Awards
and
nominations">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<div
class="rellink
relarticle
mainarticle">








Main
article:









<a
href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Bj%C3%B6rk?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="List
of
awards
and
nominations
received
by
Bj&ouml;rk">List
of
awards
and
nominations
received
by
Bj&ouml;rk</a>







</div>








<p>Bj&ouml;rk
has
received
four
awards
from
both
the
BRIT
Awards,
from
nine
nominations,
and
the
MTV
Video
Music
Awards,
from
twelve
nominations.
Bj&ouml;rk
has
also
received
13
nominations
from
the
Grammy
Awards
but
has
not
received
an
award;
she
was
nominated
every
year
from
1996
to
2002.
The
film
industry
has
also
recognized
Bj&ouml;rk
by
nominating
the
2000
song,
&quot;I've
Seen
It
All&quot;,
for
Best
Original
Song
in
a
Motion
Picture
at
the
Academy
Awards.
She
was
ranked
#36
on
VH1's
&quot;The
100
Greatest
Women
in
Rock
and
Roll&quot;
and
#8
on
&quot;MTV's
22
Greatest
Voices
in
Music&quot;.
Overall,
Bj&ouml;rk
has
received
90
awards
from
212
nominations.</p>

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Bj%C3%B6rk&page=1&ac=24&qid=3E207DC28A42742CA10FCD8E0B699BB4&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>

ask.adsPixelTimeout);








}
else
{












cb(false);








}




}
